distinguish their subtler differences; as being gifted by nature with desire to seek, patience to doubt, fondness to meditate, 
slowness to assert, readiness to consider, carefulness to dispose and set in order; and as being a man that neither affects what 
is new or admits what is old, and that hates very kind of imposture. So I thought my nature had a kind of familiarity and relation 
with truth.
